                        "><div class="casContent">There is no corresponding record for this reference.</div></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref56"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref56" class="rightTabRefNumLink">56</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit56" data-doi="10.1002/adma.201504117"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Zhang, R.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Cheng, X.-B.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Zhao, C.-Z.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Peng, H.-J.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Shi, J.-L.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Huang, J.-Q.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Wang, J.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Wei, F.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Zhang, Q.</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">Adv. Mater.</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2016</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">28</span><span class="NLM_x"> (</span><span class="NLM_issue">11</span><span class="NLM_x">) </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">2155</span><span class="NLM_x">–</span> <span class="NLM_lpage">2162</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1002/adma.201504117</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord empty" id="
                            rightTab-cas_R
                        "><div class="casContent">There is no corresponding record for this reference.</div></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref57"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref57" class="rightTabRefNumLink">57</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit57" data-doi="10.1016/j.nantod.2011.11.002"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Ji, X.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Liu, D.-Y.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Prendiville, D. G.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Zhang, Y.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Liu, X.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Stucky, G. D.</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">Nano Today</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2012</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">7</span><span class="NLM_x"> (</span><span class="NLM_issue">1</span><span class="NLM_x">) </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">10</span><span class="NLM_x">–</span> <span class="NLM_lpage">20</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1016/j.nantod.2011.11.002</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit57R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">57</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Spatially heterogeneous carbon-fiber papers as surface dendrite-free current collectors for lithium deposition</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Ji, Xiulei; Liu, De-Yu; Prendiville, Daniel G.; Zhang, Yichi; Liu, Xiaonao; Stucky, Galen D.</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Nano Today</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2012</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">7</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">1</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">10-20</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">NTAOCG</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">1748-0132</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Elsevier Ltd.</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Summary: Despite the high energy d., the lithium metal electrode has been plagued for decades with a dendrite growth problem that can result in a battery thermal runaway.  Here, we introduce anisotropic spatially heterogeneous three dimensional (3D) current collectors that prevent lithium deposition on the insulating electrolyte-facing surface and accommodate lithium deposition inside the spacious voids.  The anisotropic spatial heterogeneity was introduced by a line-of-sight deposition of a thin SiO2 layer onto a carbon-fiber paper.  The deposited SiO2 was later converted into SiC by a magnesiothermic reaction.  The SiO2 and SiC decorated 3D current collectors were confirmed dendrite-free by ex situ SEM observation after a deep lithium deposition of 28.8 C cm-2 at a high c.d. of 4 mA cm-2.  A high lithium cycling efficiency of 94% was achieved over deep deposition (14.4 C cm-2) and stripping cycles in a carbonate based org. electrolyte, demonstrating the superiority of the novel current collector for dendrite control and lithium cycling.  This strategy opens new avenues to address the dendrite problem by rationally designed current collectors and for the creation of a high energy d. electrode.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGoJR14_dU_WgbVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0ljRIh5JpzgchQ"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC38Xjt1Omtb0%253D&amp;md5=fe8ee8bead3d97a9c0eae2344d4a77e7</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref58"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref58" class="rightTabRefNumLink">58</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit58" data-doi="10.1038/ncomms9058"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Yang, C.-P.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Yin, Y.-X.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Zhang, S.-F.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Li, N.-W.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Guo, Y.-G.</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">Nat. Commun.</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2015</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">6</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">8058</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1038/ncomms9058</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit58R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">58</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Accommodating lithium into 3D current collectors with a submicron skeleton towards long-life lithium metal anodes</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Yang, Chun-Peng; Yin, Ya-Xia; Zhang, Shuai-Feng; Li, Nian-Wu; Guo, Yu-Guo</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Nature Communications</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2015</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">6</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue"></span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">8058</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">NCAOBW</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">2041-1723</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Nature Publishing Group</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Lithium metal is one of the most attractive anode materials for electrochem. energy storage.  However, the growth of Li dendrites during electrochem. deposition, which leads to a low Coulombic efficiency and safety concerns, has long hindered the application of rechargeable Li-metal batteries.  Here we show that a 3D current collector with a submicron skeleton and high electroactive surface area can significantly improve the electrochem. deposition behavior of Li.  Li anode is accommodated in the 3D structure without uncontrollable Li dendrites.  With the growth of Li dendrites being effectively suppressed, the Li anode in the 3D current collector can run for 600 h without short circuit and exhibits low voltage hysteresis.  The exceptional electrochem. performance of the Li-metal anode in the 3D current collector highlights the importance of rational design of current collectors and reveals a new avenue for developing Li anodes with a long lifespan.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGq5vVAff3FKwLVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0ljRIh5JpzgchQ"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2MXhsVKhurnM&amp;md5=8f3dc7915f87598e9c930e252db773a8</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref59"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref59" class="rightTabRefNumLink">59</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit59" data-doi="10.1021/acs.nanolett.6b01581"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Lu, L.-L.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Ge, J.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Yang, J.-N.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Chen, S.-M.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Yao, H.-B.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Zhou, F.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Yu, S.-H.</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">Nano Lett.</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2016</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">16</span><span class="NLM_x"> (</span><span class="NLM_issue">7</span><span class="NLM_x">) </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">4431</span><span class="NLM_x">–</span> <span class="NLM_lpage">4437</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1021/acs.nanolett.6b01581</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord empty" id="
                            rightTab-cas_R
                        "><div class="casContent">There is no corresponding record for this reference.</div></div></div></div></div></li></ol></li><li id="pane-m3" aria-labelledby="pane-m3" class="tab__pane tab__pane-suppInfo"><h2 class="supp-info-label">Supporting Information</h2><div class="article_supporting-info" id="rightTab-notes-1"><div class="article_content-header"><div class="article_content-header-row"><div class="article_content-title" tabindex="0"><h2 id="rightTab-_i4">Supporting Information</h2></div></div></div><hr><p class="last">The Supporting Information is available free of charge on the <a href="/" class="ext-link">ACS Publications website</a> at DOI: <a href="/doi/abs/10.1021/acs.nanolett.7b01138" class="ext-link">10.1021/acs.nanolett.7b01138</a>.</p><ul class="NLM_list-list_type-label" id="silist"><li><p class="inline">Details for experimental and characterizations; (function(){
	
	/*Event Tracking for RIS menu dropdown - Article pages*/

	$('.cit-download-dropdown_button').on('click',function(e)
	{	
		e.preventDefault();
	    gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':'Main'});

	});


	$('.cit-download-dropdown_content ul li').on('click',function(e)
	{	
	//	e.preventDefault();
	    var idx = $(this).index();
	    
	    var label = '';
	    if (idx === 0 ) {
	    	label = 'Citation';
	    } else if (idx === 1 ) {
	    	label = 'Abstract';
	    } else if (idx === 2 ) {
	    	label = 'Reference';
	    } else if (idx === 3 ) {
	    	label = 'More Options';
	    }
	   
	   gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':label});
	});

	$('.header_contnav-next a').on('click', function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Right Arrow'});
	}); 

 	$('.header_contnav-pre a').on('click', function(e){
	    e.preventDefault();
	     gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Left Arrow'});
	}); 

	$('.share_button').on('click', function(e){
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Share'});
	});

	$("#pane-m1con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Figures'});
	});

	$("#pane-m2con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
	    gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'References'});
	});

	$("#pane-m3con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Supporting Info'});
	});

	$('.tab__close').on('click', function(){
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Close'});
	}); 



})();

</script>

<script nonce="90da865f0e0cb325-SJC">
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(){
    // Function to get a Human readable formatted date
    function getFormattedDateForMaintenance() {
        let today = new Date();
        let dd = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
        //January is 0
        let mm = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0'); 
        let yyyy = today.getFullYear();
        
        let daysOfWeek = ['Sunday', 'Monday', 'Tuesday', 'Wednesday', 'Thursday', 'Friday', 'Saturday'];
        let monthsOfYear = ['January', 'February', 'March', 'April', 'May', 'June', 'July', 'August', 'September', 'October', 'November', 'December'];

        let dayOfWeek = daysOfWeek[today.getDay()];
        let monthOfYear = monthsOfYear[today.getMonth()];

        return dayOfWeek + ', ' + monthOfYear + ' ' + dd + ', ' + yyyy;
    }
    
    // Insert the date into the .system-message-date element
    document.querySelector('.system-message-date').innerText = getFormattedDateForMaintenance();
});
</script>

            //   }
            // });
            $('#gdpr-con-btn').click(function() {
                setCookie("gdpr", "true");
                hideForm();
            });
        }, time);
    }

    //Show the message
    function gdprMessage() {
        //console.log("Show GDPR Message");
        var tMessage, emailInput, messageButton, ewrap;

        $('#gdpr-message-modal').show();
    }

    function handleClick() {
        //console.log($("#gdpr-input").val());
        emailValid = validateEmail($("#gdpr-input").val());
        if (emailValid) {
            //Submit the form
            //Hide form
            if ($('.gdpr_err')) {
                $('.gdpr_err').hide();
            }

            $("#gdpr-message-content")
                //If successful then...
            setCookie("gdpr", "true");
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid + " submiting form");
        } else {
            //Show error message
            gdprErrorMessage();
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid);
        }
    }

    function gdprErrorMessage() {
        if (errorStatus) {
            return false;
        } else {
            errorStatus = true;
            $("#gdpr-message-content").append(errormessage);
        }
    }

    function validateEmail(email) {
        var re = /^(([^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+(\.[^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+)*)|(".+"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
        return re.test(String(email).toLowerCase());
    }

    function setCookie(name, value) {
        var expires = "";
        expires = "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
        document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
    }

    function getCookie(name) {
        var match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(name + '=([^;]+)'));
        if (match) return match[1];
    }

    function hideForm() { //And set cookie
        $('#gdpr-message-modal').hide();
        setCookie("gdpr", "false");
        gtag('event', 'GDPR Modal', { 'event_category': 'Pubs GDPR', 'event_label':'GDPR Dismissal'});
    }

    return {
        init: init
    }
})();

$(document).ready(infoCentralCapture.init);
</script>


                    
                        



        
        <script nonce="90da865f0e0cb325-SJC">
var currentJournal = "Nano Letters";
$(".citationLinks > a").click(function(e){
    if($(this).text() === "ACS Full Text ") {
        gtag('event', 'ACS Full Text', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Crossref") {
        gtag('event', 'Crossref', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "CAS") {
        gtag('event', 'CAS', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "PubMed") {
        gtag('event', 'PubMed', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Google Scholar") {
        gtag('event', 'Google Scholar', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).hasClass("issue-item_open-url") === true) {
        gtag('event', 'OpenURL', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
});
</script>

    console.log("ACSPubs2 start");
    $.getJSON('https://extreme-ip-lookup.com/json/', function(data, status) {
            if ( status == 'success' ) {
                $.each(data, function(i, field){

                    cookie=status;

            cookie1 = cookie;
            cookie = cookie1 + "; path=/; domain=.acs.org";

            $.cookie("ACSPubs2", btoa(cookie), {path: '/'}); // Session cookie valid across the entire site.
            //TODO send cookie val to the controller for logging

    });
});
